date: "2018-07-05"
categories: type-theory

agda: true
---

This is my attempt to collect in just one-file, a basic overview of HoTT in Agda.
This source code was type-checked by Agda 2.5.4.

{: .references }

  - https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/
  - https://mroman42.github.io/ctlc/agda-hott/Total.html

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT (`--without-K`):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="438" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="442" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="450" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="462" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="466" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="471" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="478" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="493" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="501" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#501" class="Function">_</a> <a id="503" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="505" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="509" class="Comment">-- trick for avoiding Agda module errors (jekyll)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Universes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type universe hierarchy. It hides Agda primitive
hierarchy and the keyword `Set`. It uses `Type` instead.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="782" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Universes"></a><a id="789" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#789" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="799" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="808" class="Comment">-- Our Universe hierarchy. It is implemented over the primitive</a>
  <a id="874" class="Comment">-- Agda universe hierarchy but it uses Type instead of Set, the</a>
  <a id="940" class="Comment">-- usual name for the Universe in Agda.</a>

Types
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Empty Type

The empty type, representing falsehood.

### Unit

The unit type is defined as record so that we also get the η-rule definitionally.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1843" class="Comment">-- A record without fields is the unit type with a single</a>
<a id="1901" class="Comment">-- constructor.</a>
<a id="1917" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="⊤"></a><a id="1924" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1924" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1926" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1080" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="1934" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="1942" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="⊤.★"></a><a id="1954" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1954" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="unit"></a><a id="1957" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1957" class="Function">unit</a> <a id="1962" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1964" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1954" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="1967" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1971" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> UNIT <a id="1984" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1924" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1986" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Basic types of Martin-Löf type theory and some basic
functions.

### Σ-types

Sigma types are a particular case of records, but records can be
constructed using only sigma types. Note that l ⊔ q is the maximum
of two hierarchy levels l and q. This way, we define sigma types in
full generality, at each universe.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2329" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="2336" class="Number">60</a> <a id="2339" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2428" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>

  <a id="2416" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ._,_"></a><a id="2428" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2428" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
  <a id="2434" class="Keyword">field</a>

### Products (×)

Product type as a particular case of the sigma

### Boolean

Boolean type, two constants true and false

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3082" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Bool"></a><a id="3087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3087" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="3092" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3094" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1080" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3100" class="Keyword">where</a>

* Booleans can be defined by using a coproduct.

### Natural numbers

Natural numbers are the initial algebra for a constant and a
successor function. The BUILTIN declaration allows us to use
natural numbers in arabic notation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3390" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="ℕ"></a><a id="3395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3397" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1080" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3405" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="ℕ.zero"></a><a id="3413" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3413" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="3418" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3420" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="ℕ.succ"></a><a id="3424" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3424" class="InductiveConstructor">succ</a> <a id="3429" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3431" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3433" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="Nat"></a><a id="3438" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3438" class="Function">Nat</a> <a id="3442" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3444" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="3447" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="3451" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> NATURAL <a id="3467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3469" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


### Common functions

#### Identity function
The identity function with implicit type.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="id"></a><a id="3586" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3586" class="Function">id</a> <a id="3589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3591" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3593" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3594" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3594" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3595" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3597" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3598" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3600" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3602" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3607" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3594" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3608" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3610" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3612" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3598" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3614" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3616" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3598" class="Bound">A</a>

The identity function on a type `A` is `idf A`.

some errors for my jekyll configuration.

#### Instance Searh

### Identity Type

Equality is defined as an inductive type. Its induction principle
is the J-eliminator.

### PathOver

If you have a dependent type `B` over `A`, a path `p : x == y` in `A` and two
points `u : B x` and `v : B y`, there is a **type** `[u == v [ B ↓ p]]` of paths
from `u` to `v` lying over the path `p`.  By definition, if `p` is a constant
path, then `[u == v [ B ↓ p ]]` is just an ordinary path in the fiber.
[More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L115).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="6329" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6329" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="6338" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6340" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6342" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6343" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6343" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="6346" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6348" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6350" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6351" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6351" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6353" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6355" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6343" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="6362" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6364" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6365" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6367" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6351" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6371" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6380" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6485" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="6491" class="Number">30</a> <a id="6494" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6329" class="Function">PathOver</a>
<a id="6503" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="6510" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6329" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="6527" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>

## Equational Reasoning

Equational reasoning is a way to write readable chains of equalities.
The idea is that you can write the following:

{% raw %}
```agda
  t : a == e
  t = a =⟨ p ⟩
      b =⟨ q ⟩
      c =⟨ r ⟩
      d =⟨ s ⟩
      e ∎
```
{% endraw %}

where `p` is a path from `a` to `b`, `q` is a path from `b` to `c`, and so on.
You often have to apply some equality in some context, for instance `p` could be
`ap ctx thm` where `thm` is the interesting theorem used to prove that `a` is
equal to `b`, and `ctx` is the context. [More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L270).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7201" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="EquationalReasoning"></a><a id="7208" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7208" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="7228" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7229" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7229" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7231" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7233" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7234" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7234" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7238" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="7243" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7229" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7245" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7247" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="7256" class="Comment">-- Common combinators for equational reasoning. They allow us to</a>
  <a id="7323" class="Comment">-- write proof in an equational style. These versions have been</a>
  <a id="7389" class="Comment">-- adapted from the old version of the HoTT-agda library.</a>

<a id="7753" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="7758" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7208" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Actions on paths I

Properties and structure of the equality type.

### Equality

Types are higher groupoids.  If we see equalities as paths, this
is the inverse of a path. If we see equalities classically, this
is the symmetric property of equality.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="inv"></a><a id="8057" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8057" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8061" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8063" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8065" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8065" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8066" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8068" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8069" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8069" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8071" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8073" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8078" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8065" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8079" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="8082" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8083" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8083" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8085" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8085" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8087" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8089" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8069" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8090" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="8094" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8096" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8083" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8098" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8101" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8085" class="Bound">b</a>
  <a id="8105" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8107" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8085" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8109" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8112" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8083" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="8114" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8057" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8118" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8119" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5213" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8124" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8124" class="Bound">a</a><a id="8125" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8127" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8129" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5213" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8134" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8124" class="Bound">a</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Functions are functors to equalities.  In other words, functions
preserve equalities.

## Properties on the groupoid

<a id="9838" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9843" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8943" class="Module">·-Properties</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Transport

When we transport a proof of `(P a)` over an equality `(a == b)`, we
get a proof of `(P b)`.

                <a id="14204" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14206" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14207" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14207" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="14209" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14211" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14143" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14213" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14216" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14145" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14217" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14219" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14221" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14222" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14222" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14224" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14226" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14153" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14228" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14143" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14230" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14232" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14171" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14234" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14143" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14235" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Homotopy

In a type-theoretical sense, a homotopy between two
functions is a family of equalities between their applications.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14692" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="14699" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14699" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="14708" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14709" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14709" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14712" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14712" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14714" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14716" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14717" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14717" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14719" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14721" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14726" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14709" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="14728" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14730" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14731" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14731" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14733" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14735" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14717" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14737" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14739" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14744" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14712" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14746" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14748" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14756" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="14834" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="14874" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14874" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14883" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14885" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14886" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14886" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14888" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14888" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14890" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14892" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14894" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14894" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14896" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14898" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14717" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14899" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14901" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14903" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14731" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14905" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14894" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14906" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14909" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14911" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14916" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14917" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14709" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14920" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14922" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14712" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14924" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14874" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14937" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14937" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14939" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14939" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14941" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14943" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14944" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14944" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14946" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14948" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14717" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14949" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14951" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14953" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14937" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14955" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14944" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14957" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14960" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14939" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14962" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14944" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="Homotopy._∼_"></a><a id="14967" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14967" class="Function Operator">_∼_</a> <a id="14971" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14973" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14974" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14974" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14976" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14976" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14978" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14980" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14982" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14982" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14984" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14986" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14717" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14987" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14989" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14991" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14731" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14993" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14982" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14994" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14997" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14999" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="15004" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15005" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14709" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="15008" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15010" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14712" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="15012" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15016" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15016" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15018" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14967" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15020" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15020" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15022" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15024" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14874" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="15033" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15016" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15035" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15020" class="Bound">g</a>

  <a id="15040" class="Comment">-- Homotopy is an equivalence relation</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.h-refl"></a><a id="15081" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15081" class="Function">h-refl</a> <a id="15088" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15090" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15091" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15091" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15093" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15095" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15096" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15096" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15098" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15100" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14717" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15101" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15103" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15105" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14731" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15107" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15096" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15108" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15110" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15112" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15091" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15114" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14967" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15116" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15091" class="Bound">f</a>

## Naturality

Homotopy is natural, meaning that it satisfies the following
square commutative diagram.

A particular case of naturality on the identity function.

## Fibers

## Equivalence

    <a id="18321" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="18389" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="18454" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="18471" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18471" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="18482" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18484" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18485" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18485" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18487" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18489" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18284" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18491" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18493" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18298" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18494" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18496" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18498" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18503" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18504" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18276" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18507" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18509" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18279" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18511" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="18565" class="Comment">-- There exists an equivalence between two types if there exists a</a>
    <a id="18636" class="Comment">-- contractible function between them.</a>

## Cartesian Product

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="21988" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="CartesianProduct"></a><a id="21995" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21995" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a> <a id="22012" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22013" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22013" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="22016" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22016" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22018" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22020" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22021" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22021" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22023" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22025" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22030" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22013" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="22032" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22034" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22035" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22035" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="22037" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22039" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22044" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22016" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22046" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22048" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="22057" class="Comment">-- In a pair, the equality of the two components of the pairs is</a>
  <a id="22124" class="Comment">-- equivalent to equality of the two pairs.</a>
  <a id="CartesianProduct.prodComponentwise"></a><a id="22170" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22170" class="Function">prodComponentwise</a> <a id="22188" <a id="22902" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="22907" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21995" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## DecidableEquality

A type has decidable equality if any two of its
elements are equal or different. This would be a particular
instance of the Law of Excluded Middle that holds even if we do not
assume Excluded Middle.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="23173" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DecidableEquality"></a><a id="23180" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23180" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="23198" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23199" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23199" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23200" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23202" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="23211" class="Comment">-- A type has decidable equality if we can prove that any two of its</a>
  <a id="23282" class="Comment">-- elements are equal or different.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEq"></a><a id="23320" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23320" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23326" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23328" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23329" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23329" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23331" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23333" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23338" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23199" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23339" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23341" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23343" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23348" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23199" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="23352" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23320" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23358" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23358" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23360" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23362" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23363" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23363" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23365" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="23367" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23358" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23370" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23372" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23374" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23375" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23363" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23377" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23365" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23381" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23383" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2901" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="23385" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1675" class="Function">¬</a> <a id="23387" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23363" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23390" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23365" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23394" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="23399" class="Comment">-- The product of types with decidable equality is a type with</a>
  <a id="23464" class="Comment">-- decidable equality.</a>

<a id="23885" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="23890" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23180" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Propositions

Propositions as described on the main text. A type
is a proposition if we can create a function making any two of its
elements equal. We create a type of propositions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="24120" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="24127" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24127" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="24140" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24149" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
  <a id="24218" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="24233" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24233" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24242" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24244" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24244" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24245" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="24248" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24249" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24249" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24251" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24253" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24258" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24244" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24259" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24261" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24263" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24268" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24244" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="24272" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24233" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24279" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24279" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24281" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24283" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24285" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24285" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24287" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24287" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="24289" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24291" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24279" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24292" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24294" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24296" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24285" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24298" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="24301" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24287" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24302" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24307" class="Comment">-- The type of mere propositions</a>
  <a id="Propositions.hProp"></a><a id="24342" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24342" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24348" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24350" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24352" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24352" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24353" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24355" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24357" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24362" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24363" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="24368" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24352" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24369" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24342" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24379" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24380" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24381" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24383" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24385" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2350" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24387" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24380" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24394" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24396" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24233" class="Function">isProp</a>


  <a id="24407" class="Comment">-- The dependent function type to proposition types is itself a</a>
  <a id="24473" class="Comment">-- proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.piProp"></a><a id="24491" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24491" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24498" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24500" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24502" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24502" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24505" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24505" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24507" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24509" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24511" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24512" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24512" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24514" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24516" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24521" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24502" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24523" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24525" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24527" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24528" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24528" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24530" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24532" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24512" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24534" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24536" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24541" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24505" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24543" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="24554" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24556" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24558" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24558" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24560" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24562" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24512" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24563" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24565" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24567" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24233" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24574" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24575" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24528" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24577" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24558" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24578" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24581" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24583" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24233" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24590" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24592" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24592" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24594" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24596" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24512" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24597" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24599" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24601" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24528" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24603" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24592" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24604" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24608" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24491" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24615" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24615" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24621" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24621" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24623" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24623" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24625" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24627" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20318" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="24634" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24636" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24636" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24638" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24640" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24615" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24646" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24636" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24648" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24649" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24621" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24651" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24636" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24652" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24654" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24655" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24623" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24657" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24636" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24658" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24663" class="Comment">-- The product of propositions is itself a proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp-prod"></a><a id="24721" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24721" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="24733" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24735" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24737" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24737" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24740" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24740" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24742" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24744" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24746" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24747" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24747" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24749" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24751" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24756" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24737" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24758" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24760" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24762" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24763" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24763" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24765" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24767" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24772" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24740" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24774" class="Symbol">}</a>
              <a id="24790" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24792" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24233" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24799" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24747" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24801" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24803" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24233" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24810" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24763" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24812" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24814" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24233" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24821" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24822" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24747" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24824" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2726" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="24826" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24763" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24827" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24831" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24721" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="24843" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24843" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="24845" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24845" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="24847" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24847" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24849" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24849" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="24851" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24853" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22317" class="Function">prodByComponents</a> <a id="24870" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24872" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24843" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="24874" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="24876" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="24879" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2428" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="24881" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24882" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24845" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="24884" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="24886" class="Symbol">_))</a>

<a id="24891" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24896" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24127" class="Module">Propositions</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Sets

Sets are types without any higher dimensional structure, all
parallel paths are homotopic and the homotopy is given by a
continuous function on the two paths.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25104" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Sets"></a><a id="25111" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25111" class="Module">Sets</a> <a id="25116" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="25125" class="Comment">-- A type is a &quot;set&quot; by definition if any two equalities on the type</a>
  <a id="25196" class="Comment">-- are equal.</a>

  <a id="25250" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25212" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25256" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25256" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25258" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25260" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25261" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25261" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="25263" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25263" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="25265" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25267" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25256" class="Bound">A</a><a id="25268" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25270" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25272" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24233" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="25279" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25280" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25261" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="25282" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="25285" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25263" class="Bound">y</a><a id="25286" class="Symbol">)</a>

             <a id="25472" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25474" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25212" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25480" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25430" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25482" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25212" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25446" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25492" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25494" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25212" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25500" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25501" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25430" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25503" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2726" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="25505" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25446" class="Bound">B</a><a id="25506" class="Symbol">)</a>

     <a id="25560" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25543" class="Bound">p</a>

<a id="25811" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="25816" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25111" class="Module">Sets</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## HLevels

Higher levels of the homotopical structure, where the
first levels are:

- Contractible types (0)
- Propositions (1)
- Sets (2)

They would correspond to homotopy levels. We only work with
these first levels.

## EquivalenceProp

Equivalence of two types is a proposition
Moreover, equivalences preserve propositions.

<a id="28079" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28084" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27297" class="Module">EquivalenceProp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Half-Adjoints

Half-adjoints are an auxiliary notion that helps us
to define a suitable notion of equivalence, meaning that it is a
proposition and that it captures the usual notion of equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28328" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Halfadjoints"></a><a id="28335" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28335" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="28348" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28349" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28349" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28352" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28352" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28354" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28356" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28357" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28357" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28359" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28361" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28366" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28349" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="28368" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28370" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28371" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28371" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28373" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28375" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28352" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28382" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28384" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="28393" class="Comment">-- Half adjoint equivalence.</a>
  <a id="28424" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Halfadjoints.ishae"></a><a id="28431" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28431" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="28437" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28438" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28438" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28440" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28442" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28357" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28444" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28446" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28371" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28447" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28449" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28451" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28456" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28457" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28349" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28460" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="28462" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28352" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28464" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28466" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="31006" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="31011" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28335" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Quasiinverses

Two functions are quasiinverses if we can construct
a function providing gfx = x and fgy = y for any given x and y.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31185" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Quasiinverses"></a><a id="31192" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31192" class="Module">Quasiinverses</a> <a id="31206" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31207" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31207" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="31210" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31210" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31212" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31214" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31215" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31215" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31217" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31219" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31224" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31207" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="31226" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31228" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31229" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31229" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="31231" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31233" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31238" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31210" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31240" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31242" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="33938" class="Comment">-- Half-adjoint equivalences are quasiinverses.</a>

     <a id="35402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2444" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35406" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35407" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35015" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="35414" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35329" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35415" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35417" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4058" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="35419" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2444" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35423" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35329" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="35429" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7546" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="35433" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20318" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="35440" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35441" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19587" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="35457" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35329" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35458" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35460" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7546" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="35467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3586" class="Function">id</a>
   <a id="35473" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7645" class="Function Operator">∎</a><a id="35474" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="35477" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="35482" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34223" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Univalence

Voevodsky's univalence axiom is postulated. It induces
an equality between any two equivalent types. Some β and η rules
are provided.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="35681" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Univalence"></a><a id="35688" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35688" class="Module">Univalence</a> <a id="35699" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="35743" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="UnivalenceAxiom"></a><a id="35750" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35750" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="35766" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35767" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35767" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="35768" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35770" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35771" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35771" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35773" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35773" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="35775" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35777" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="35782" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35767" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="35783" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35785" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="36485" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="36490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35750" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="36506" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Somme lemmas about Univelance

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="36584" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36587" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceLemmas {ℓ} where</a>
<a id="36626" class="Comment">--     -- The identity equivalence creates the trivial path.</a>
<a id="36687" class="Comment">--     ua-id : {A : Type ℓ} → ua idEqv == refl A</a>
<a id="36736" class="Comment">--     ua-id {A} =</a>
<a id="36755" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="36770" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv              ==⟨ ap ua (sameEqv (refl id)) ⟩</a>
<a id="36835" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (refl A)) ==⟨ ua-η (refl A) ⟩</a>
<a id="36888" class="Comment">--         refl A</a>
<a id="36906" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="36917" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36920" class="Comment">--     -- The composition of equivalences is preserved into composition</a>
<a id="36992" class="Comment">--     -- of equalities.</a>
<a id="37017" class="Comment">--     ua-comp : {A B C : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → (β : B ≃ C) → ua (compEqv α β) == ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37113" class="Comment">--     ua-comp α β =</a>
<a id="37134" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="37149" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α β)                               ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv x β)) (inv (ua-β α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37256" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) β)                ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) x))</a>
<a id="37361" class="Comment">--                                                            (inv (ua-β β)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37440" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β))) ==⟨ ap ua lemma ⟩</a>
<a id="37516" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))                     ==⟨ ua-η (ua α · ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37599" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37622" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="37633" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="37648" class="Comment">--         lemma : compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β)) == idtoeqv (ua α · ua β)</a>
<a id="37734" class="Comment">--         lemma = sameEqv (</a>
<a id="37763" class="Comment">--           begin</a>
<a id="37782" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua β)) ∘ fst (idtoeqv (ua α))                 ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="37870" class="Comment">--             (transport (λ x → x) (ua β)) ∘ (transport (λ x → x) (ua α)) ==⟨ transport-comp (ua α) (ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37980" class="Comment">--             transport (λ x → x) (ua α · ua β)                           ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="38068" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))</a>
<a id="38111" class="Comment">--           ∎)</a>
<a id="38127" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38130" class="Comment">--     -- Inverses are preserved.</a>
<a id="38164" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua α · ua (invEqv α) == refl A</a>
<a id="38244" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r α =</a>
<a id="38264" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="38279" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua (invEqv α)      ==⟨ inv (ua-comp α (invEqv α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="38349" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap ua (compEqv-inv α) ⟩</a>
<a id="38414" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv                  ==⟨ ua-id ⟩</a>
<a id="38463" class="Comment">--         refl _</a>
<a id="38481" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>

<a id="38495" class="Comment">--     ua-inv : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua (invEqv α) == inv (ua α)</a>
